		writefile_2();

}

		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') != '07ff4a9413979deb32a4e0780500455c45cc4858') {

	}

				warn('Creation of backup failed');

			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/viathinksoft/raPages/092_invite/OIDplusPageRaInvite.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_12();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/raPages/092_invite/OIDplusPageRaInvite.class.php') !== '0349ae197fed010dec2f8991118266b682a30bad') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/raPages/092_invite/OIDplusPageRaInvite.class.php');
		}
	}
}
